 Homophones aise shabdon ko kehete hai jinke uccharan to ek jaise hote hai lekin matlab alag- alag
 This is the reason why most of us use homophones incorrectly
 angreji bhashaa main yun to bahut se Homophones hai lekin aam bolchaal main kuch shabdon kaa istemaal khub hota he
 Know which are those words - 1
 there-their-they'rethere: yah vaakya main Pronoun or an adverb kii tarah istemaal hota he
 (we went to Paris and stayed there for ten days) His: Pronoun (everyone has their own way of doing things
 )they're: Contracted version of they are (they're happy)
 2
 accept-exceptaccept: yah ek Verb he, jiskaa matlab he kisi cheez ko apnaanaa
 (give her a little time toacceptthe idea) Except: It is Preposition, which means to separate or exclude
 (I didn't tell him anything,except thati needed the money)3
 lose-looselose: This word is used when something is lost
 (tonight, Ilosehim forever)loose: kisi cheez ke sahi bhang se feet nahin hone par iskaa prayog kiya jaataa he
 (the dog gotlooseand ran out of the yard
 )4
 it's-itsit's: it is written to use it is or it has
 (it'scold in here
 ) Its: It is a possessive form (I really like the way that car looks, butitsprice is more than i can afford
 )5
 bear-barebear: Either the animal or a verb
 Meaning is to carry or support
 (I could notbearto see her punished
 - yahaan shabd kaa arth bardaasht karne se he
 ) Bare: Not being clothed or covered (don't go out inbarefeet - ie don't go out barefoot) 6
 carat-caret-carrotcarat- sone kii shuddhta maapne ke liye prayog kiya jane vaala shabdancharet- kisi line ke neeche banaaya jane vaala nishandchharrot- ek prakaar kii sabji7
 to-two-tooto- This is preposition
 (I am going to the store
 ) two-number Too- This is Adverb, which means 'also' (also)
 (I can see you too
 ) 8
 week-weakweek- saptaah(i am going home this week
 ) Weak- Weak from the body (you are looking very weak today
 )9
 prey-prayprey-hunting (we should pray to God atleast one time in the day)
 )10
 weather-whetherweather-weather (weather is not good today) Whether- Expressing a doubt, I'll see whether she's at home) 11
 then-thanthen-yah adverb he, jise ection ke samay prayog kiya jaataa he
 (first you tie your laces and then run
 )than-yah conjunction he, jiskaa prayog tulana ke liye kiya jaataa he

 cricket ke sabase sampurna ballebaajon main se ek bharat ke purv openar sunil gavaskar ne inke liye kabhi kaha tha ki, 'jahir ab bas karo'ji haa ham baat kar rahe hai apane daur se sabase khatarnaak ballebaajon main se ek rahezhir abbaaski
 Know some big things related to him on the occasion of his becoming ICC President
 1- 100 pratham shrenee shatak banane vaale pehle asian
 2- Debutted in 1969 and scored 274 runs in the second match against England, which is still the fourth highest Test score for Pakistan
 3- abbaas ne apane kariyar main kul chaar dohare shatak jamaaye, itihaas main sirf 10 ballebaajon ne unase zyada dohare shatak jamaaye hai
 4- Only second batsman with Geoffrey Boycott making his hundredth first class century in a Test match
 5- chaar baar kisi pratham shrenee match main shatak or doharaa shatak jamaane vaale iklaute khilaadi
 And he remained unbeaten in these eight innings
 6- 1981-82 or 1984-85 main pakistan kii captaini bhi kii
 7- played for Gloucestershire in county cricket for 13 years
 jisamen unhone 49

 glucestershire ke liye lagbhag har saal hi 1000 se zyada ran banane vaale abbaas ne county cricket main do baar 2000 se bhi zyada ran banaae
